  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c903139d-ca96-41cc-875d-2ff74c0c27ca'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

Men and women alike fall into his bed—after all, Logan is not one to discriminate. He lives by one motto—if something interests you, why not just take a chance and try?<br /><br />And he wants to try Tate Morrison.<br /><br />Just coming out of a four-year marriage with an ex-wife from hell, a relationship is the last thing on Tate’s mind. He’s starting fresh and trying to get back on his feet with a new job at an upscale bar in downtown Chicago.<br /><br />The only problem is, Tate has caught the unwavering and unwelcome attention of Mr. Logan Mitchell – a regular at the bar and a man who always gets what he wants.<br /><br />Night after night Tate fends off the persistent advances of the undeniably charismatic man, but after an explosive moment in the bar, all bets are off as he finds his body stirring with a different desire than his mind.<br /><br />As arrogance, stubbornness and sexual tension sizzles between the two, it threatens to change the very course of their lives.<br /><br />Logan doesn’t do relationships.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer651884832" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15523132808202487746">You know what I love about this book?<br/><br/>The hype! No really, I love it. <br/><br/>I'm thrilled that an m/m book is attracting so much attention and enticing a whole lot of new curious hetero readers to explore the genre. I absolutely love that, and for that reason I really, really wanted this book to be a shiny sparkling example of what new readers can expect from this genre. Ella Frank is not an author I have read before but she comes with a reputation for writing good hetero erotica and so I thought if Joe</span>
  <span id="freeText15523132808202487746" style="display:none">You know what I love about this book?<br><br>The hype! No really, I love it. <br><br>I'm thrilled that an m/m book is attracting so much attention and enticing a whole lot of new curious hetero readers to explore the genre. I absolutely love that, and for that reason I really, really wanted this book to be a shiny sparkling example of what new readers can expect from this genre. Ella Frank is not an author I have read before but she comes with a reputation for writing good hetero erotica and so I thought if Joey W. Hill (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5709572.Rough_Canvas__Nature_of_Desire___6_" title="Rough Canvas (Nature of Desire, #6) by Joey W. Hill" rel="nofollow noopener">Rough Canvas</a>) and Kele Moon (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16002547.Starfish_and_Coffee" title="Starfish and Coffee by Kele Moon" rel="nofollow noopener">Starfish and Coffee</a>) can pull off the switch so beautifully why not give her a chance.<br><br>Ella Frank’s first mistake is to not being able to let go of the hetero by including a graphic m/f sex in the first paragraph – a big no-no! <i>“her creamy thighs where spread wide apart with his cock sliding in and out of her soaking wet pussy” </i>is not something that appeals to the typical m/m reader. Yes 80% of us are woman and yet, I do sympathise for the 20% who are GAY men. Is it not polite to mention somewhere in the blurb that this book contains scenes of graphic m/f sex? Not (according to some) necessary, but I do feel it is courteous and respectful. If the roles were reversed I suspect there would be uproar.<br><br>Try is a gay-for-you erotic story – that’s it - there is nothing else, no surprises, no angst, no humour, no plotline – want and possession – that is all. Logan is the bisexual initiator and Tate is the confused straight guy. The two men circle each other in a dance that’s predictable push and pull with dialog that is uninspired - full of clichéd sexual innuendos like this …<br><br><i>“You’ll be hungry then? Logan: Yes, but not for food. Tate?”</i><br><br>Not only is the dialog clichéd, it’s very questionable. What man actually says things like <i> “All of that <u>honey-colored skin, naked under me, your curls all over my pillow </u>as I drive my cock inside you—oh yeah, Tate, that’s going to happen. Mark my words.”</i> - This is not realistic.<br><br>The conversation is so borderline cheesy and without weight that I never connected to either of these MC’s, they are simply too simple, too fictional and shallow. How old are they? Why is Tate a barman, did he not get a college education? All I know is their petty high school jealousies and the need for constant (girly) reassurance. No matter how many times (at least 49!!) I am reminded of their physical attributes I found them uninspiring; together they fired up about as much chemistry as a bowl of milk.<br><br>This book is labelled erotica and yes there is a lot of sex. But each scene is like a copy of a copy of the scene before it – the mechanics might change but the descriptive is the same: rigid cocks, molten kisses, groans and growls, up against the wall, biting lips, heated stares, mine blah-blah-blah. I really couldn't care about a 20 page blow job scene that might as well have been performed by a woman. I was bored while Ella Frank worked her way down her list, ticking every off each sexual act to eventually reach a point of ultimate surrender. For me this writer does not capture the true essence of what m/m erotica is and her effort pales in comparison to what this genre has to offer. But then, your mileage may vary …<br><br>I slump and can only hope that Ella’s fans will enjoy this one as much as they enjoy her previous works. I want to embrace all these brave new readers and welcome them into the genre with open arms but I fear that this book not a good representation at all. So please believe me when I say that in comparison this book really <s>sucks</s> is the poor relation.<br><br>I find myself bitterly disappointed with this book. All of it. It feels so far removed from m/m romance that I could scream and weep for the genre’s missed opportunity. I’m sorry I have to be the droll policeman standing in front of the spotlight of shiny gif excitement waving a hand and repeating “Nothing to see here folks, move along ….this way please” and points to the recommendation list below.<br><br>To the new m/m reader:<br><br><a href="http://boysinourbooks.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Boys in Our Books </a>recommend these books as a great place to start your m/m journey:<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13420351.Shattered_Glass__Shattered_Glass___1_" title="Shattered Glass (Shattered Glass, #1) by Dani Alexander" rel="nofollow noopener">Shattered Glass</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10506237.Hot_Head__Head___1_" title="Hot Head (Head, #1) by Damon Suede" rel="nofollow noopener">Hot Head</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6080449.Deadly_Nightshade__Deadly_Mystery___1_" title="Deadly Nightshade (Deadly Mystery, #1) by Victor J. Banis" rel="nofollow noopener">Deadly Nightshade</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7493186.Promises__Coda_Books___1_" title="Promises (Coda Books, #1) by Marie Sexton" rel="nofollow noopener">Promises</a>)<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4801582.Faith___Fidelity__Faith__Love____Devotion___1_" title="Faith &amp; Fidelity (Faith, Love, &amp; Devotion, #1) by Tere Michaels" rel="nofollow noopener">Faith &amp; Fidelity</a>)<br><br>This genre has SO MUCH MORE to offer you, SO MUCH! If you loved this book then m/m is going to rock your world - if you didn’t love it? I don’t blame you. This is NOT a good introduction (IMO) but don’t give up yet.<br><br>Honestly, you don’t know chemistry until you have read books by the likes of Abigail Roux, Anne Tenino and Aleksandr Voinov, and if you want great m/m erotica? We recommend anything by Heidi Cullinan or Cameron Dane. There are so many more wonderful authors like Brandon Shire and Tom Webb that offer heartfelt, beautiful descriptive prose and genuine quality to call on.<br><br>For the devout m/m readers: There really is nothing to see here, you have read it all before. I cannot recommend this book to anybody.<br><br> <br><a href="http://boysinourbooks.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405828i/791124.jpg" alt=" photo PersonalizedBannerShelley_zpsa7c55832.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15523132808202487746" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_639239151" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639239151" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/639239151?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer639239151" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7468989074317611384"><b>5 Fantastic Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/3dda55fa-8c01-4c9c-b4af-12655d7276a3_zps068a4123.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384150745i/6794188.jpg' alt=' photo 3dda55fa-8c01-4c9c-b4af-12655d7276a3_zps068a4123.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>Try</i> is Ella Frank’s first go at an m/m novel, and I feel that she knocked it out of the park. I really loved the characters, the humor, the steam, just everything about this one!<br/><br/> After reading <i>Edible</i>, I knew I needed more of Cole’s half brother and partner at his law firm, Logan. When Logan Mitchell first sees new bartender Tate Morrison, it is lust at first sight. Logan doesn’t know if Tate is gay or straight, and Logan could care less. When he wants someone, he wants them</span>
  <span id="freeText7468989074317611384" style="display:none"><b>5 Fantastic Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/3dda55fa-8c01-4c9c-b4af-12655d7276a3_zps068a4123.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384150745i/6794188.jpg" alt=" photo 3dda55fa-8c01-4c9c-b4af-12655d7276a3_zps068a4123.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Try</i> is Ella Frank’s first go at an m/m novel, and I feel that she knocked it out of the park. I really loved the characters, the humor, the steam, just everything about this one!<br><br> After reading <i>Edible</i>, I knew I needed more of Cole’s half brother and partner at his law firm, Logan. When Logan Mitchell first sees new bartender Tate Morrison, it is lust at first sight. Logan doesn’t know if Tate is gay or straight, and Logan could care less. When he wants someone, he wants them. He doesn’t do relationships, but he likes to Try a bit of everything. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“So... I like to try a bit of everything and everyone.”</blockquote>
</i><br>Tate is a newly divorced bartender. He has never been attracted to a man, but there is something about Logan. The way he looks at Tate, pursues him. He wants no part of this thing with Logan, but his body can’t deny the attraction he feels towards him. All Logan wants is for Tate to take a chance. To just try.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/ffda7993-81f9-44d4-9536-7aecbb077175_zpsc3efeeb0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384150745i/6794189.jpg" alt=" photo ffda7993-81f9-44d4-9536-7aecbb077175_zpsc3efeeb0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The build up and sexual tension between Tate and Logan was great. I loved watching Tate’s internal struggle between what his head was telling him he should want, and what he actually wanted. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“It’s like you expect me to flip a switch and just accept that everything I ever believed about myself has changed, and that I should be okay with that. Do you know how insane that is?” <br>“I do. But do you know what else is insane?”<br> “What?” <br>“You still haven’t told me no.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/9d08b94e-ffcd-469c-b627-a06ff27e6290_zps76a78794.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384150745i/6794190.jpg" alt=" photo 9d08b94e-ffcd-469c-b627-a06ff27e6290_zps76a78794.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“I want you as hot, hard, and desperate as you’ve ver been before- and once you’re there... then I’ll take you.”</blockquote>
</i> In my opinion, Logan Mitchell was the shining star in this book. I couldn’t get enough of this guy. He’s confident in who he is and what he wants. He’s sexy as all get out and so funny to boot! Some of my favorite Logan lines- <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>Just when he figured life was going to be easy and hand him a woman to bend over his desk, it threw him a nice fucking curve. <br>Batter up! I want to play with some balls.<br><br>“Yes, I know that was inappropriate. But, Tate?” <br>“Yes, Logan?”<br> “That’s when I’m at my best.”<br><br> “Boundaries, Logan. I think you’ve crossed enough with me today.” <br>“We’ve also established that I have none.”<br><br>“Give you an inch...”<br> “And I’ll want six or seven more.”<br><br>“You’re so fucking big.”<br> “Words no man minds hearing ever.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>All humor aside, Logan had an internal struggle in the story as well. He wanted Tate, but he wants a lot of people. Sex is easy for him, it’s everything else thats difficult. Tate is the first person in a long time to make him want to try something different. To make him want more than just the fun and meaningless sex he’s used to. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“You make me want things that I’d forgotten I wanted.” </blockquote>
</i> <a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/14cb3443-9141-4a76-af44-32b6a5ef8877_zpsf8550f93.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384150745i/6794191.jpg" alt=" photo 14cb3443-9141-4a76-af44-32b6a5ef8877_zpsf8550f93.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tate and Logan change each other. Bring out new wants, needs, and desires. <br><br><br>Sexy, intriguing, funny and sweet. The chemistry that Logan and Tate shared was off the charts hot! And the humor and back and forth witty banter was great. I loved Logan and Tate together in all ways. This is a must read! I highly recommend it for those who love m/m, and for those who haven’t read any, this would be the perfect title to start with. Just give it a try. I’m so excited for book 2- <i>Take</i>. I think we will get to see even more of Logan and Tate’s character development and watch their relationship grow. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/8bd22ec5-d037-4be8-949d-cb0d9679f28e_zpsbafbf795.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384150745i/6794192.jpg" alt=" photo 8bd22ec5-d037-4be8-949d-cb0d9679f28e_zpsbafbf795.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Every time we do this, it convinces me that I’m exactly where I need to be.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><br><i>***ARC kindly provided by author, Ella Frank in exchange for an honest review***</i></span>

I have read all her books and I thought she couldn’t top Blind Obsession. Oh well, hello Tate & Logan! You guys sure gave Philippe a run for his money.<br/><br/>If you guys check the blurb you’ll know what this book is about, I won’t talk a lot about the story, this will be about my feelings when I was reading the book.<br/><br/>I need to say I was excited when I heard Ella was writing her first MM book. I know some </span>
  <span id="freeText6468803829786277226" style="display:none"><br><br><b>T</b>empting<br><b>R</b>aw<br><b>Y</b>ummy<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383833573i/6679938._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Try is the first MM book by Ella Frank and I sure as hell hope is not the last one. I have read all her books and I thought she couldn’t top Blind Obsession. Oh well, hello Tate &amp; Logan! You guys sure gave Philippe a run for his money.<br><br>If you guys check the blurb you’ll know what this book is about, I won’t talk a lot about the story, this will be about my feelings when I was reading the book.<br><br>I need to say I was excited when I heard Ella was writing her first MM book. I know some of you guys are reluctant when MF authors decide to write MM but I guess we need to <b>TRY</b> their books before judging, right? So I added it to my TBR without even knowing what this book was about. When I read the blurb and realized this was about a “straight” guy I was happy dancing in my desk. Yes, I love GFY stories, I can’t freaking help it and let me tell you this, ELLA FREAKING DELIVERED!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383775672i/6663774.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is a light and hot as hell read and even though I am not a huge fan of erotica lately, I loved this one. We have two completely different male characters. We have Tate who is a confused bartender who crosses paths with Logan, a lawyer who will make him question his own sexual tastes. <br><br>But what happens when you think you know everything about yourself and suddenly you start questioning your feelings? Are you able to accept it or will you fight against yourself?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383775672i/6663775.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You need to read the book to know what happens but trust me when I say this is a book that will make you feel those butterflies in your tummy. I loved the banter between them, I loved how they were fighting each other with their words but they were eye fucking each other with their eyes. You could cut the sexual tension between them.<br><br>And yeah, this book only spans over two weeks of their relationship so you guys need to have this into account. I absolutely HATE reading books where characters love each other after one kiss or one quick fuck. That’s NOT real. So I am very grateful that Ella stuck to reality and showed us a real relationship during their first two weeks. I can’t wait to get into more emotional stuff in the next book.<br><br>That being said, I must also admit there were two emotional moments that were completely outstanding for me: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ their moment in the kitchen when they intertwined their fingers and that TERRIFY ME moment that is my absolutely FAVE part of the book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And the most important thing, Ella has a huge number of ‘MF readers’ fans who are willing to give this genre a <b>TRY</b>. That is just AMAZING, I can’t wait for them to discover how completely AWESOME is this genre.<br><br>I can’t wait to <b>TAKE</b> that second installment, my body is more than ready for more Tate &amp; Logan. <br><br>So, are <i>you</i> ready to <b>TRY</b>?<br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer687684381" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4475113759578365825">**2.5 stars**<br/><br/>I had no idea what to expect with this book. My M/F reader friends pretty much all loved it and my M/M reader friends pretty much all hated it. I am a hard-core M/M lover with hundreds of M/M books under my belt. I honestly was prepared to hate this fully and completely. <br/><br/>Surprisingly, I didn't. But you might. <br/><br/>Does this book work as a convincing romance? <b>No.</b> The main characters literally spend no time getting to know one another. None. Logan is a pushy jerk and Tate is practically fo</span>
  <span id="freeText4475113759578365825" style="display:none">**2.5 stars**<br /><br />I had no idea what to expect with this book. My M/F reader friends pretty much all loved it and my M/M reader friends pretty much all hated it. I am a hard-core M/M lover with hundreds of M/M books under my belt. I honestly was prepared to hate this fully and completely. <br /><br />Surprisingly, I didn't. But you might. <br /><br />Does this book work as a convincing romance? <b>No.</b> The main characters literally spend no time getting to know one another. None. Logan is a pushy jerk and Tate is practically forced into each step of his "relationship" with Logan. I hated Logan. I thought Tate and Logan were horrible together. I didn't get them at all as a couple and I thought it was not convincing at all. <br /><br />However...<br /><br />As a M/F author, I had expected Ella Frank to be... well, shy about M/M sex. I haven't read any of her books before this one and I though it would be tentative for some reason. I was knocked off my feet by the amount of graphic sex in this one. <br /> <br />And so...<br /><br />Well, I have this kind of fetish, as some of you might know. I love, LOVE "sexuality discovery" books. Give me a gay virgin and I'm as happy as can be. So even though the sex was more than a bit cheesy at times, I have to say, I LOVED that part of the book. I could have read about hesitant, drawn-out first-timer sex all day long. I wish the couple actually WORKED together, but... you know... details ;) <br /><br />I was going to round down to 2 stars but I'm so pleased that so many readers are trying M/M from this book that I rounded up to three stars. And if any first time M/M readers are reading this review and want some recs, please hit me up! I have a whole new world to show you. ::Cue "Aladdin" music::</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=did-not-finish">did-not-finish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=m-m-romance">m-m-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=gay-for-you">gay-for-you</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer827651574" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10155385918674420057"><b>DNF’d at 48%</b><br/><br/>Oh dear. At least,<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417139130i/12237290.jpg' width='400' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This book was too excessively hot. And I mean it: TOO HOT. Not in a good way. The repetitive sex was omnipresent, past the sexual tension in the first chapters, and it annoyed the hell out of me.<br/><br/>Not at first though. Oh, not at all. When Logan met Tate, I was <em>oh so hooked</em> and clutching my tablet hard as if I thought that would make me even more connected to the whole story and everything inside it.<br/><br/>I LOVED the beginning: overconfident, cocky and full of libido Logan m</span>
  <span id="freeText10155385918674420057" style="display:none"><b>DNF’d at 48%</b><br><br>Oh dear. At least,<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417139130i/12237290.jpg" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book was too excessively hot. And I mean it: TOO HOT. Not in a good way. The repetitive sex was omnipresent, past the sexual tension in the first chapters, and it annoyed the hell out of me.<br><br>Not at first though. Oh, not at all. When Logan met Tate, I was <em>oh so hooked</em> and clutching my tablet hard as if I thought that would make me even more connected to the whole story and everything inside it.<br><br>I LOVED the beginning: overconfident, cocky and full of libido Logan met ‘straight,’ perplexed and curious barman Tate. The sexual tension and dialogs that followed are unforgettable and kept making me grin. Logan’s bluntness is hilarious, smirk-worthy and totally riveting.<br><br>And so they discussed, flirted, flirted, flirted, argued, flirted and then things got even more steamy.<br><br>Which wasn’t bad.<br><br>The first sex scenes were <em>to die for</em> and I couldn’t wait to read more of them here and there, when fitting the events that I assumed would follow.<br><br>But there were no events. No plot. Barely a conflict. Barely any secondary characters. Way more sex scenes than welcomed. Way more flirting and dirty talk than necessary.<br><br>Don’t get me wrong, I don’t mind erotica at all, but I cannot read a book that is too focused on something – sex – and has its plot neglected. It simply got boring and predictable.<br><br>Had the book somehow ended at 45% of its story or so, I would have given it at least a four star rating, that’s for sure. But it didn’t. So I can’t. This is a pattern I have observed with M/M romance stories: they’re usually slow because they put focus on the couple, they have great and intense sex, and an atmosphere that goes right to the feels. But the long ones – three hundred pages plus – tend to get repetitive and rarely held any surprises, after a good amount of pages. That’s how it goes with M/Ms for me. Doesn’t mean that I will never encounter exceptions though. But this is not one of them, apparently.<br><br>Also, it’s like Tate had a considerable character development from the first to the last chapter I have read. At first, he was calm, a little cocky and definitely chattier with people. But, he then started showing this temper, bluntness that matched Logan’s and a bit of a too alpha-like personality, while Logan submitted…<br><br>Strikingly, it started out so well but the ride changed roads without my approval.<br><br>Definitely a ‘love or hate’ type of book. Sigh, I am more than disappointed at how it turned out for me, but let’s hope this book will feel different to you!<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10155385918674420057" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I want you. Tell me how I can have you.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><u>Books in The Temptation Series should be read in order:</u><br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/758893167" rel="nofollow noopener">Try</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/764788100" rel="nofollow noopener">Take</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/636543543" rel="nofollow noopener">Untitled</a></b><br><br><b>Try (book 1) is the story of successful attorney and man-whore extraordinaire Logan Mitchell in his pursuit of Tate Morrison, a straight bartender fresh out of a divorce</b>. <br><br>After work Logan likes to stop by the bar downstairs to pick up men and/or women for casual sex. One night <b>he spots a new bartender and decides he wants him - at all cost and so his relentless flirtation, seduction and taunting of Tate begins</b>. After his divorce Tate is not looking for a relationship with another woman, much less a man. He just likes to flirt a little with customers to ensure a good tip, but he is <b>quickly unsettled by Logan</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I don’t care if I have to be here every fucking night. I’m going to have him.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>This story is as very much a <b>seduction with sexual tension</b> out-of-this world, but it is also a <b>story of self-exploration and dealing with one’s past</b>, for both Logan and Tate. And naturally the story will touch on the <b>subject of prejudices</b>. I think the title is indicative of the theme as it was a <b>journey of “Try’s” for both of them</b>.<br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/dg24BWbysb_zps89279840.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Logan, Logan who can resist him? Seven words to describe <b>Logan Mitchell: Complex, captivating, jaded, dominant, relentless, flawed and…. vulnerable </b>.<br><br><a>

</a><br><br>Three words to describe <b>Tate Morrison: Conflicted, reflective, loyal, noble, insecure, endearing and sincere</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“You make me want things that I’d forgotten I wanted.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>The build-up of sexual tension kept me glued to my Kindle</b>. That said, the dialogue felt a bit off/slow at times and their little spats made me question their ages (which I don’t believe were revealed in book). <b>As for ending</b>…. it leaves them in a good place, but with several unresolved issues. It is clear that there is much more of their story to come!<br><br><b>Off-the-charts sexual tension! Charismatic and memorable characters! An interesting and compelling journey and a very enjoyable read!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b> I’m going to enjoy making you pay for that particular cocktease.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>

  <span id="freeText16777525694614133841" style="display:none"><b>5 Sexy Steamy Stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384373253i/6859982._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>"You know what you want to do. There's no one here, and no one is going to come in. Just do it,” he whispered, "Try."</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384193213i/6809627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ella Frank's books need to come with a damn warning.<br><br><b>Reader beware: Contents of book are extremely hot</b><br><i>Please read at your own risk...<br>Side effects may include:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383767601i/6660809.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> TOA: Total Ovary Annihilation<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383767601i/6660809.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> The constant need to attack your significant other<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383767601i/6660809.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> A constant and persistent Hot and Bothered sensation<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383767601i/6660809.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> The repercussions of having to take care of said Hot and Bothered sensation if significant other is unavailable</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384375904ra/6860714.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384193213i/6809627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I had pretty high expectations for this book when I first found out about it. Especially since it was right around the time I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16249388.Edible__Exquisite___3_" title="Edible (Exquisite, #3) by Ella Frank" rel="nofollow noopener">Edible</a>, which I friggin LOVED! I couldn't wait until Ella's foray into the MM genre. But I was almost afraid to read this, thinking I may have set my hopes a little too high. Well disappointed, I was not. I loved the hell out of this book! Try was one hot fucking ride, (pun most definitely intended) that I didn't want to end.<br><br>If you're looking for a deep and emotional story, that's not quite what you'll get here. I think my BR pal Allison had it right with it being 90% sex and 10% story. But you know what? I was VERY OK with this. It wasn't mindless smut, it had just enough story to keep the reader engaged and begging for more. Given that this is book 1 out of 3, I'm thinking we'll get a whole lot more story in the next books.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384193213i/6809627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I knew I would love Logan after the quick intro we get of him in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16249388.Edible__Exquisite___3_" title="Edible (Exquisite, #3) by Ella Frank" rel="nofollow noopener">Edible</a>, and I was definitely right. The man was just delicious. The things that would come out of his mouth? He had me worked up with every dirty and outrageous word that would leave his mouth.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384193213i/6809628._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"Does every word that comes out of your mouth have to do with sex?" <br>"Usually, eighty/twenty, but with you, it seems more ninety-eight/two."<br>"And the other two?" <br>"The other two I have spent trying to convince you."<br>"And do you think I’m convinced?" <br>"I think you’re getting there.' <br>"And when I do? What happens to the two percent? More sex?"<br>"I think when you get there, you’ll never want to leave. One thing about guys—we like sex. How long has it been, Tate? I’ll give you the best sex you've ever had." </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384193213i/6809628._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384375953ra/6860719.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tate was the perfect ying to Logan's yang. I loved how hard he tried to resist Logan. But let's be honest, how can anyone possibly resist Logan for long? The man is damn persistent when he knows what he wants. He's not shy about voicing his desires, and he was definitely desiring Tate.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384193213i/6809628._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">This? This changes things. If you think I’m going to walk out of here and you’ll conveniently forget about what happened, you should think again. This wasn't a fluke, no matter how much you try to pretend. You wanted it as much as I did, and you should remember that tonight when you jerk off, thinking about my tongue in your mouth."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384193213i/6809628._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And when these two get together?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384285107ra/6837157.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I thought my Kindle just might spontaneously <b>cum</b>bust. Holy fucking hot cock, batman!<br><br>I think I might have highlited every single thing that came out of Logan's mouth. I sat there for hours trying to pick and choose quotes for my review, and at the end, I pretty much gave up. Everything he said is pure gold, and I think I'd have a never ending review even if I gave you just a few of my favorites. So this is all she wrote...<br><br>For those that are afraid of a cliffy<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The end was very satisfying with a HFN scenario. There was no major cliffhangers that will drive you batshit waiting for book 2 to be released.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Miss Frank,<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/623797.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>You are the queen of steam. I cannot wait to see what book 2 will bring.<br><br>Thank you to all my awesome BR buddies! Nothing like popping a few MM cherries to make for one EPIC Buddy Read ;)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/1567724-try--epic-br-and-mm-cherry-popper?page=7#comment_86743183">https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/...</a><br><br>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <span id="freeText13143534000294122075" style="display:none"> <b>5 HOT SEXY STARS</b><br><br> OMG WOW THIS BOOK IS AMAZING!!<br><br>This book totally hooked me from the first page until the end!!!<br>I love Ella's writing and with this challenge writing a M/M she proves how great author she is!<br>This is my first M/M from a woman author and I didn't know what to expect...Ella didn't disappoint me!!Try is amazing!!!<br><br><b>"There's no one here and no one is going to come in. Just do it,"<br>"Try." </b><br><br>Logan is a confident, sexy and arrogant guy who likes sex and he doesn't care if it's with women or men…He isn't the monogamous type and the only thing he wants is to have fun!!<br>Until he meets… the new bartender who works at Logan’s favorite after work spot.,,<br>The only thing Logan wants is to have this man in his bed...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383945591i/6713190.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tate…mmmm he is gorgeous and divorced...but the fun is that he is straight!!<br>But he is intrigued from Logan...He can't understand what he really feels...and afraid to Try anything...with Logan<br>Can Logan manage to make Tate Try things that are unusual for him????<br>When they are finally together things start being more serious...they want more than only sex...<br>Can they manage to keep their relationship?? <br>There are problems that they must tide over...<br><br>Wow <br>I loved the chemistry between them from the beginning!!These two have a passionate connection! <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384215312i/6816714._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is really hot and steamy!!!For me it's one of the hottest books I have ever read!! <br>I fell in love with the boys!!!I like Logan's smart mouth <br><br><b>"Tate you're sexy as fuck.The minute I saw you,I got hard.When you opened your mouth,I became one hundred percent interested.And when you kissed me?I lost my damn mind.I'll be as patient as I need to get you inside me." (omg Logan *sigh*)</b><br><br>and Tate…well I like everything about him!<br><br>I can't wait for Take!<br><br>Thank you so much Ella and Rosalinda!!<br><br>*arc kindly provided by author, Ella Frank in exchange for an honest review*<br><br>IT'S LIVE!!<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00GM2GOW8/ref=cm_cr_rev_prod_title">http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00G...</a></span>

It feels like I waited forever for the next Ella Frank book to come out. I am so in love with Logan and Tate. Their bantering was fabulous, the aggression between them was always </span>
  <span id="freeText8830826952295286461" style="display:none">I was going to write over my previous posts in my review but I'm too fond of it to let it go. So I shall just add on to it. It feels like I waited forever for the next Ella Frank book to come out. I am so in love with Logan and Tate. Their bantering was fabulous, the aggression between them was always sexual no matter how mad one of them may have been at the other. Leading me to believe that this book had some of the hottest angry sex ever!!! It was wonderful watching Tate and Logan grow both separately and together as they each had their own battles to fight while trying to figure out if they could make it work. JUST WOW!!!!!!!!! Get it! I wouldn't change a single sentence, a single word, a single comma! I'm a newbie in the M/M Romance world, but <i>Tate and Logan</i> just made it into my all-time favorite book couples, so there's <b>THAT</b>... This book will be one of those that I reread a 1000 times like a lunatic and enjoy immensely every f*cking time, for sure. <br><br><i>** A special THANK YOU to all of my GR buddies that recommended this awesomeness to me after learning I've recently popped my M/M cherry. <b>YOU GUYZ ROCK</b> and I seriously f*cking love you all! **</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405336432ra/10383461.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Logan Mitchell</u>
</b> has always had the same motto: <i>Try/Take/Top.</i> In other words, <i>“Try a sample, take the goods, and then come out on top and NEVER LET THINGS GET MESSY.”</i> He is a <b>successful lawyer with a fat wallet</b> and a <b>pretty face</b> that -along with his <i>“milkshake”</i>- brings <i>“all the girls and boys to the yard”</i>, …<b>if you know what I mean... ;)</b> He has no desire to bind himself to someone, oh no, he wants to <b>TRY</b> a little bit of everyone, <i>man or woman</i>, that interest him enough and when his interest wanes…<i>just move on to his next prey.</i><br><br>But the rules of the game change when <b>Logan</b> walks into his favorite bar next door to his Office and catches a glance of<i> beautiful brown curls framing a masculine face</i> belonging to the new bartender, <b>Tate</b>…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424128521ra/13719692.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Tate Morrison</u>
</b> is a <i>VERY</i> straight guy on the verge of an ugly divorce with the wife he just couldn't keep happy whatever he’d done over the years and all he wants is <i>some alone time</i> to get his life back on track.<br><br>But a <i>set of blue eyes peering back at him behind black hipster glasses</i> and the <i>very flirtatious words</i> exchanged with the owner of them make that task impossible… <b>Logan</b> is one of the regulars of the bar <b>Tate</b> has started working at 2 days ago as a bartender, and <b>Tate</b> isn't sure how to feel about the guy's gaze always following him around…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381499638ra/4948695.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u><b>Logan</b> can’t get the bartender out of his mind.</u> The potent need to <b>TRY</b> this easygoing and relaxed guy that gets incredibly tense and unsettled <i>only when around <b>Logan</b></i>, is suffocating. Logan always goes after what he wants and he is going to have <b>Tate</b>, there’s no doubt about that.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Considering you seemed so confused when, really, there is nothing to be confused about.”<br><br>“Except for the fact that I’m <u>STRAIGHT.</u>”<br><br>“Yes, well, I don’t let <u>LITTLE</u> things like that stand in my way.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430624ra/863444.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But there’s a surprise waiting for <b>Logan</b> this time… <b>Logan Mitchell</b> who is always the one on charge, who has never wanted or pursued a man as hard before, who has never waited for anyone, turns into a nervous wreck ready to beg for more whenever he is near <b>Tate</b>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You've changed me, and you don't even realize it. Just being with you, near you? It makes me want to be a BETTER person. You make me want to take a RISK.”<br>~ LOGAN</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418866281ra/12926596.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u><b>Tate</b> can’t get the blue-eyed devil out of his mind.</u> This guy is too pushy, too arrogant, too confident and his smart mouth pisses <b>Tate</b> off…<b>all while giving his c*ck the most intense ache it has ever experienced.</b> As much as he wants to yell that he doesn't even <i>LIKE</i> <b>Logan</b>, there’s no fooling anyone since his body says otherwise… Yes, <b>Tate Morrison</b>, a man that has never had a doubt about being straight in his life, has a hard-on for a guy! And more importantly: <b>He is okay with this fact.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I want the man who sat down across from me and changed the way I look at the world. And if that’s WRONG, then I’m confused because when I’m near you, it feels <u>SO DAMN RIGHT.</u>” <br>~ TATE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/492021.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u><b>Tate</b> gives a good fight</u> but he can’t resist <b>Logan</b>’s charm much longer... But can he even trust a man that constantly switches his <i>“choices”</i>? How can he hold his hand and take a step into the unknown when it’s all about the the <i>“chase”</i> for the man in question? What if he gets what he wants, gets bored of him and leaves him with his world crushed?<br><br><u><b>Logan</b> gives a good fight</u> and finally gets what he wants… But is he even willing to <b>TRY</b> and push past his fears to keep <b>Tate</b> around, when the idea of tying himself to anyone <i>terrifies</i> him? How can he do all that, when the man in question is acting like he is embarrassed by <b>Logan</b> and wants to remain <i>“secret friends”</i>? How can he swallow up his hurt and bravely <b>TRY</b> to keep this man in his palms?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“So...what's your truth, Logan?”<br><br>“I think <u>YOU ARE.</u>”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392059154ra/8494074.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>P.S:</u>
</b> Sorry about the overabundance of HAWT HAWT HAWT gifs....I couldn't help myself ;)<br><br>OFF TO BOOK#2! ♥<br></span>

    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1203198458?book_show_action=true">Feb 17, 2015</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34846729-try">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=lgbt">lgbt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=humour">humour</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=best-of-2016">best-of-2016</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1203198458" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8118428040344211039"><i>Spoiler-free review for Try, Take and Trust!</i><br/><br/><b>5++ **<u>my kindle just caught fire</u>** STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458738569i/18524755.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There's no one here and no one is going to come in. Just do it,” he whispered, eyes locked on to conflicted brown orbs, “Try.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I...this book...this series...Logan...Tate...speechless. <br/><br/>We throw things like binge reading around quite liberally. When I say I couldn't put these books down I actually mean it. Three days with no more than three hours of sleep per night. I got absolutely nothing done in the </span>
  <span id="freeText8118428040344211039" style="display:none"><i>Spoiler-free review for Try, Take and Trust!</i><br><br><b>5++ **<u>my kindle just caught fire</u>** STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458738569i/18524755.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There's no one here and no one is going to come in. Just do it,” he whispered, eyes locked on to conflicted brown orbs, “Try.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I...this book...this series...Logan...Tate...speechless. <br><br>We throw things like binge reading around quite liberally. When I say I couldn't put these books down I actually mean it. Three days with no more than three hours of sleep per night. I got absolutely nothing done in the meantime. I was lost in this scorching hot and incredibly addictive love story between Logan and Tate. Goes right on my all-time-favourite and best-of-2016 shelves. Simply unbelievable.<br><br>The level of hotness was almost ridiculous, riddled with constant innuendos, sexual tension jumping off the page and I've been grinning like a loon ever since.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389543630ra/8039038.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re pretty pissed off, Tate. What’s wrong? Afraid you might like it? How do you know unless you try?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>The Temptation Series</i> is a gay for you M/M story.<br><br><b>Tate Morrison</b> just came out of a bad relationship and is in the process of putting his life back together and divorcing his soon to be ex-wife. He is straight. Never even thought about being with a man. That is until his second day of working behind the bar at After Hours when he serves this guy...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429416378ra/14585234.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Hmm…mouthy lawyer equals one sexy cocksucker.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Logan Mitchell</b> is a thirty-four year old lawyer who lives by the motto to try everything at least once. Women. Men. Doesn't really matter. He is the most over the top flirt and to be perfectly clear - a man-whore. Logan has no boundaries, no filter whatsoever and he goes after what he wants. That being Tate, the sexy bartender. <br><br>What follows is a sizzling cat and mouse play between Logan and Tate. The poor guy never stood a chance when it comes to the counselor.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458639612ra/18510935.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What can I say? The series is addictive. Logan and Tate stole my heart. The banter, initial courting, up until they really commit to one another was golden. I love the characters. The polar opposites that attract and somehow fit together like they were made for one another. Logan’s unapologetic brazenness and Tate’s silent strength was just pure magic for me. Not to mention they are so damn sexy together. <br><br>Over the course of three books Logan and Tate deal with a lot of issues. Starting with the fact that Tate is actually straight. Fortunately Logan is relentless in his pursuit. While they get over the fight with themselves there are other problems adding up. Family, prejudice, sexual exploration and the ultimate commitment to each other.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You make me crazy and furious and out of my mind with need, but in the end, you make me so fucking happy. I can’t ever remember feeling this way. And no one is going to tell me it’s wrong. No one.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The thing that really sold me right from page one was the deep connection. The first moment Logan and Tate meet the spark between them is palpable and overtime such a strong bond and intimacy develops. It was simply beautiful to see their relationship blossom beyond the physical attraction and against all odds. All of that is done in a very detailed way in dual POV and with a lot of very descriptive and panty melting sex scenes. Which in no way means lack of growth emotionally or the absence of plot. It's just REALLY sexy, well and it is erotica after all. So no complaints from me.<br><br>The <i>Temptation Series</i> is something to lock out the world and get lost in for a few days. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411425866ra/11226000.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm not big on reading M/M books. For no particular reason I just never was drawn to them. But almost all my GR friends have recommended this series to me and I have to say it was a huge win and not unlike Tate I feel like I have been corrupted. Male on male might not be for everyone, but I truly believe the kind of love Logan and Tate have for each other transcends gender and is just epic.<br><br>On top of that the writing is stellar and captivating. Ms. Frank rather effortlessly sucks you in and she sure won't let you go until you're done. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I want the man who sat down across from me and changed the way I look at the world. And if that’s wrong, then I’m confused because when I’m near you, it feels so damn right.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Only question left is. Why on earth haven't I read this earlier? Seriously? I honestly think there is nothing hotter on my bookshelf. If you haven't read the series or even tried one of Ms. Frank's books, I don't know what you are doing. She is an author to check out for sure.<br><br>In conclusion...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Congratulations,” Logan heard whispered as Tate’s hand snaked down between them, and his fingers wrapped around him. <br><br>“On?” he pushed past the lump in his throat. Tate raised his head and looked him right in the eye.<br><br>“Corrupting me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458639612ra/18510936.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm still shocked, all kinds of turned on and a little lost. Book-hangover material if I ever saw one.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447539995i/17017465.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_664481303" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/664481303" />
    <a title="Sara " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5058304-sara"><img alt="Sara " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1439650883p2/5058304.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/664481303?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara " href="/user/show/5058304-sara">Sara </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer664481303" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2373690522828464539">So when you hear that a traditional male/female romance writer is diving in the male/male genre you are curious. When you hear that it’s an author that has a dedicated following you are a bit excited that they will be introducing their fans to the wonderful genre that you are saturated in and loving. When you get the book, you are confused from page one when the MC is balls deep into a wet pussy. Oh yeah. I had to check the blurb before I went on to make sure this was about two DUDES and not som</span>
  <span id="freeText2373690522828464539" style="display:none">So when you hear that a traditional male/female romance writer is diving in the male/male genre you are curious. When you hear that it’s an author that has a dedicated following you are a bit excited that they will be introducing their fans to the wonderful genre that you are saturated in and loving. When you get the book, you are confused from page one when the MC is balls deep into a wet pussy. Oh yeah. I had to check the blurb before I went on to make sure this was about two DUDES and not some sort of ménage or just a bisexual deal. Nope. Okay then, let’s see where this goes.<p>

</p><p>Where this went was downhill fast. The MC’s were not likeable, Logan was arrogant to the point I wanted to punch him in the throat and Tate was so wishy-washy I rolled my eyes so much I could see yesterday. Cheesy lines, you say? Oh yeah. How can my brain not go there after struggling through 300+ pages of I don’t know what the hell that was? Can someone help me, please?</p><p>We are told how to feel as these men test the waters of their relationship. I never figured out why either of them liked the other. I get it; they are both hot yet other than Logan’s constant reenactment of a Robin Thicke summer hit wearing Tate down, I don’t understand why he went for it. Logan is supposed to be some sexy alpha man whore whose milk shake brings everyone to the yard…um, I never saw the appeal. The story was all over the place, it was awkward and did not have a steady flow. The abundance of details may suit some but not me, nor does repetitiveness and good lord the dialogue drove me nuts. Did the inner goddess come over for tea with the boys? I was so tired of reading the word TRY in every tense it could be in. I couldn’t bring myself to do a search count for it, I did not want to see it again. Can we say over usage at its finest?</p><p>Now, I get that this will have an audience and the audience it is intended for… I am not a ticket holder of. I currently read strictly m/m romance, I am lost in it and I love it. From boys figuring out their sexuality to gay for you stories, to FBI agents to hard core BDSM. The boys do it for me and <b>they are boys.</b> Now, if you haven’t read m/m romance you won’t understand that there IS A DIFFERNCE in how it’s written. It’s not just a search and replace him for her or penis for vagina. It’s different. Men are different. They have sex different, they interact different, they think different. This read to me as men thinking like women would. They had sex like women would. Yes, anatomy aside, it read as women in the scenes. Along with that misstep, there was zero connection between the MC’s. I did not feel they were into each other at all. Scenes that should have had me full of emotion had me irritated to the point I wanted to give up and DNF this at 30% but I have liked previous work from the author and know what she is capable of. Unfortunately, this fell short. Hell, this didn’t even pull out the toddler stool to see onto the m/m shelf. It was just off, so off when it had a chance to be a bridge between the two genres.</p><p>With all the hype and pre-release reviews out there already I will expect this to have glowing ratings. I will be the odd chick out and that is fine. Regardless of where I get a book, I am honest about my reading experience. I am sure the reader this was intended for will love it and that is as it should be. This just was not for me.</p><p>
  <a></a>
  <br />
  <i>*ARC provided by the author for an honest review*</i>
</p></span>

    <a title="Exina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5309539-exina"><img alt="Exina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580809437p2/5309539.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/965518480?book_show_action=true">Jun 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Exina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Exina" href="/user/show/5309539-exina">Exina</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=undeveloped-romance">undeveloped-romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer965518480" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14423088519848334214"><i>*DNF at 52%</i><br/><br/>Based on the hype I expected an extraordinary, wonderful and heart-wrenching story… so I expected a romance. But it is <b>NOT a romance.</b><br/><br/><b>It is a (badly recited) chronicle of a seduction.</b> Logan sets eyes on Tate and wants him in his bed. He is used to get everything whatever he desires, but Tate resists him. Tate’s resistance sets Logan afire, and makes him even more insistent. (Oh, see how nicely I can paraphrase ‘stalkerish’… lol)<br/><br/>Tate is attracted to Logan – for whatever reason –but he i</span>
  <span id="freeText14423088519848334214" style="display:none"><i>*DNF at 52%</i><br><br>Based on the hype I expected an extraordinary, wonderful and heart-wrenching story… so I expected a romance. But it is <b>NOT a romance.</b><br><br><b>It is a (badly recited) chronicle of a seduction.</b> Logan sets eyes on Tate and wants him in his bed. He is used to get everything whatever he desires, but Tate resists him. Tate’s resistance sets Logan afire, and makes him even more insistent. (Oh, see how nicely I can paraphrase ‘stalkerish’… lol)<br><br>Tate is attracted to Logan – for whatever reason –but he is straight, and freaked out by lusting for a man. <br><br>So this is <b>the conflict</b> they’re constantly and repeatedly talking about and thinking about. <b>No plot, no palpable emotions, no characterization.</b> The only question is if they‘ll fuck or not. And as it is labelled as an erotica story, you already know that they will. <br><blockquote>
  <i>Hesitantly, he pushed forward. “What else do you… like about me?” <br>“Like? That’s not the right word.” <br>“Then, what word would you use?” <br>“What else turns me on about you?” Logan suggested.</i>
</blockquote><br><b>The characters</b> are not likeable. Logan is irritating and stalkerish, Tate is irritating and pathetic. We hardly know anything about them, but their looks are depicted exhaustively. <br><br><b>The writing style</b> is awful, full of repetitions. The author’s favorite phrase seems to be “That was when…”. It occurs 25 times. You think I’m exaggerating? See this:<br><blockquote>
  <i>that was when he’d seen Jessica<br>That was when the bartender gave<br>that was when he came to his final conclusion<br>That was when Tate had backed off.<br>that was when Tate’s reality became one huge<br>That was when Cole jumped in.<br>That was when he curled his fingers<br>that was when Tate decided he needed to get the<br>That was when Logan’s expression went from<br>that was when Tate decided to join in on the<br>That was when a low laugh hit his ears.<br>That was when he also discovered<br>That was when he realized that<br>That was when he got to watch<br>That was when Logan stopped<br>that was when he spoke up.<br>that was when he found himself promising,<br>That was when Logan lost his patience.<br>That was when he heard a question<br>That was when Red slid down<br>that was when it hit him.<br>That was when Tate felt someone<br>That was when Logan stepped back,<br>That was when Logan’s palms smoothed<br>that was when the sound of his cell phone</i>
</blockquote><br>The other is “that was what”. <b>I didn’t even dare to count the word “try”. Fitting title, huh?</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>“What’s wrong? Afraid you might like it? How do you know unless you try?”</i>
</blockquote><br>I hated the games they played, hated the shitty, repulsive and unnecessary M/F sex scenes.<br>The <b>M/M erotic scenes</b> were equally bad too: boring, repetitive, and drowsy. No intensity, no chemistry. <br><br>Sometimes (okay, okay… often) I love a steamy and dirty PWP story, but it was not like that. All the steam of the world would have been evaporated due the elongated sex scenes, the all-present and endless conversations about the same thing over and over again. <br><br>I really don’t get the high ratings. <br><br>Recommended? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407774561ra/10763621.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14423088519848334214" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

He never thought that after having people fall into his bed that the one person he wanted wouldn't do that. He had to pursue Tate, something he doesn't do. The only thing that bugged me at times about Logan, was that he couldn't be serious when Tate wanted to be. But at the same time, I kind of liked it, it was very confusing to me. There were many times I wanted Logan to <i>TRY</i> with Tate. He asked so much of Tate and I wanted him to as well when Tate asked that of him. But he would get scared, which was understandable, but I wanted him to take that final leap. Other than that, I really loved him.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384389005i/6864191._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tate Morrison is currently trying to finally end his four year marriage with his ex-wife who is trying to make things difficult. Tate isn't interesting in dating at the moment and is perfectly content on his own. He's trying to start anew. He is living in a small apartment and just got a job as a bartender. Tate is charming and gorgeous but he is also straight. And when he meets Logan, there is something about him that catches his attention. Tate goes through a journey of trying to come to terms with that, he just needs some time. I totally got where Tate was coming from, I can understand his initial shock and hesitancy to agree to Logan's proposal. But I loved that once he gave into his feelings, he was able to be more confident in himself and what he was doing. I liked that he gave back to Logan just as much as what he recieved. Yes, he was unsure at times, and more than a little terrified, but this was all new to him. I like that Tate was open minded and that he slowly tried things out with Logan. I wouldn't have believed it if things went too fast. I loved the every interaction Tate had with Logan. And I loved it when Tate's sexy side would come out.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384389214ra/6864225.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>

There was just a lot of heat between these characters. I know this is an erotica, so of course there is going to be a lot of sex in this book. I will admit that even though the sex was über HOT, I kind wanted more of a relationship to happen between them, for more of their emotions to come out to light. But that was because I had thought initially going in that this was a stand alone. I hadn't realized it was part of a three book series where Tate and Logan's story would continue. Now, I SERIOUSLY can't wait to read the next book. It seems that emotional connection I was craving for them will finally come in the next book. Ella totally left me hanging with that ending. There was a bit of a cliffhanger (but not really, in the sense that things did get resolved at the end). So it did leave you with an overall good feeling. But it did leave you wanting a whole lot more. It was a great debut m/m novel from Ella Frank. As per usual, the sex scenes were the best and really well written. I enjoyed the characters very much. Again, I can't wait to read more of these two. Loved it!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*Part of the EPIC Buddy read*</span>

</a><br><br><b>
  <br>
  <blockquote>"You know what you want to do. There's no one here, and no one is going to come in. Just do it,” he whispered, "Try." </blockquote>
</b><br><br>Devoured this book. Logan is relentless in his pursuit of Tate. He's so arrogant but Tate brings out a whole different side to Logan. He's never had a relationship, doesn't stick around but this guy makes him want more...<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=4f55ac794acc4803e140212f964e8cbd_zps0c513944.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384434894i/6875574._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If you've never ventured into the MM scene, this is a great cherry popper. This was a big buddy read and A few girls had never read this genre. The book is seriously hot but there's a love-story here too. I think the whole GFN thing makes delving into it easier for non-seasoned MM readers. It's angsty and a slow build. Not a quick wam-bam, thank you maham. Logan keeps trying for Tate but Tate resists so by the time he caves to Logan's advances, you're screaming your release, "Yes!"<br><br><a href="http://reactiongifs.com/?p=10124" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420026ra/833110.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=557476df0afb5c5caee49bd4ae5c2a1f_zps2a03db6c.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384434894i/6875575._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tate doesn't share. Can Logan commit to an exclusive relationship? Both are entering uncharted territory here. Tate never being with a man, Logan never having a relationship beyond sex. Can they make this work?<br><br>So, considered yourself warned. Find your spouse, significant other, WHATEVER you need to get through this sizzling book. It is seriously panty melting hot. <br><a href="http://reactiongifs.com/?p=14720" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384435386ra/6875617.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Looking forward to the future books about Logan and Tate. <br><br>Thanks for the awesome buddy read ladies! Even though I took up the rear! (Pun entirely intended)</span>

When he sees something he likes, he gets it. <br><br><i>

How his past shaped the man that he is today. There is far more depth to Logan yet to be explored and something tells me that beyond the hard shell, the sexual innuendos and all the flirting; Logan is going to blow us away. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384141889i/6790275._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>But things are going to get real messy. </i> <br><br>There is just something about Logan that causes Tate to react. First it’s his eyes that can’t seem to stay off of him, then his thoughts and eventually it’s his the rock hard cock nestled between his legs. Tate’s never wondered what it would be like to be with a man, but something about Logan makes him want to <i>try</i>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384141889i/6790276._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This was a fantastic. I had moments in this story where I was certain that I was going to explode from the sexual tension between these two. She teases us until we are going to explode and then she gives it to us good. And when these two finally get there, hold on tight. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384141889i/6790279.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I devoured this book. I fell even more in love with Logan and his smart mouth and Tate, well he just fucking owns me. Since I can’t really compare this to other m/m books I can only say that this lived up to every prior book from Ella Frank. My first scenes that involved m/f/m had taken some time to get accustomed to, but there was never a moment in this where I was mentally trying to throw a vagina into the mix, well okay… maybe I was mentally inserting my vagina into a few of the scenes… <br><br>I cannot wait for Take to be released to see where there story goes. Is Logan finally ready to give up his sexual freedom? Is Tate ready to accept that who he wants is a man? I hope that someone has secured Ella to her chair and has an IV drip of coffee going so that we can get our obsessive and greedy hands on these two soon. A must read for fans of m/m books or anyone that is an Ella Frank fan. If you were like me and never ventured down this road before, this is the perfect introduction. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381984454i/5509956._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422561ra/840987.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/565243.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
