  <span id="freeText3662697085889100627" style="display:none">One thing I really hate about Goodreads is pre-release fangirl-squeeing!<br />The book page looks like a flashing advertising pillar, or - as my friend stated it so nicely - someone ran amok with gifs of nekkid men.<br />Is that supposed to make me want to buy the book? And who is Ella Frank?<br />I`m not one of Pavlov`d dogs...<br /><br /><b>Edit 11/12<br />DNF</b><br /><br /><br />Apparently I am - so many pics and gifs and squees - my siren call for an honest review - books pushed like this are NEVER good....(and I was told the review above isn`t a review...well, duh!)<br /><br />Let`s say curiosity won.<br />I read the extract downloaded from Amazon - three chapters - and I really, really don`t have to read on.<br />Chapter two and three were slightly altered variations of the first and I doubt very much that will change.<br />The Story has - so far - NO plot, NO worldbuilding, ZERO character development.<br />What I got was the generic arrogant asshole (Logan) who sticks his dick in every willing orifice, may it be female, male, furry, or battery operated, just to get his rocks off. (Apparently this sort of male character is hot shit in m/f romance, but PLEASE don`t ask me why...)<br />All I know about his newest erotic challenge (Tate) is that he`s straight, gets divorced and has the nervous habit to wipe down the counter.<br />So far just het-sex with breast wiggling females drooling over dicks - a mere decoration to put m/f readers at ease, I guess.<br />Sexual tension between the male characters? I was told it`s there but I didn`t feel it - not a single, tiny spark.<br />Don`t let me start about the dialogue - these men think and talk ONLY with their little brains - is this supposed to be erotic?<br /><br />And...there is no "and"...that was it. In one word - bland!<br /><br />This might have been written as a bridge between m/f and m/m - admittedly not a bad idea and with good intentions - at least I hope so.<br />Sorry to say it passes that goal with flying colours.<br />I don`t know what quality in books m/f readers are used to, or what they require from an erotic romance but for most m/m readers this strange hybrid might be a disappointment.<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=november-reads">november-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer718493758" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15779979070600606594">PHEW! What a smoking hot read this was! I am rating this 4.5 sizzling stars!!! Let's face it folks; Ella Frank can write a sex scene like its nobody's business! She wrote the scenes so well, that most of the time I forgot it was male/male and supposedly somewhat forbidden! I pretty much forgot the fact that they were two males and just got sucked right in to two people who were sharing extremely hot intimacy with one another. That is one of the main reasons I feel this would be a perfect book fo</span>
  <span id="freeText15779979070600606594" style="display:none">PHEW! What a smoking hot read this was! I am rating this 4.5 sizzling stars!!! Let's face it folks; Ella Frank can write a sex scene like its nobody's business! She wrote the scenes so well, that most of the time I forgot it was male/male and supposedly somewhat forbidden! I pretty much forgot the fact that they were two males and just got sucked right in to two people who were sharing extremely hot intimacy with one another. That is one of the main reasons I feel this would be a perfect book for anyone who is hesitant to try a male couple book. The other reason is that Tate, who is one of the main characters, is learning too! So, what a perfect way for the reader to become aquainted with the M/M genre; to learn right alongside the hero!<br /><br />For readers that aren't familiar with Ella Frank's other series, Logan was introduced as Cole's step brother back in Edible. Logan and Cole are Lawyers and have their own firm together. After work Logan likes to mosy on down to the After Hours pub for a drink to unwind. Oh yes, I must add that he is what I consider a manwhore! Most people know it too, especially the staff that work at the pub; because let's face it, he has had sex with pretty much the whole employee roster! One night when Logan goes their for his drink, he comes across a new bartender. This would be Tate, the hot curly brown haired stud! As you can imagine Logan's radar goes off, and he wants Tate--BADLY! There is a wee problem though, and that would be that he is pretty dang sure that Tate is straight.<br /><br />Now for most individuals this would be a road block that you just do not cross..*snort* NOT for our dear Logan! Oh no, this bump in the road just makes him more determined to have Tate. Let the games begin. These two begin to have verbal sparring matches that are so highly amusing, and in Logan's case highly inappropriate that it is impossible to notice the growing attraction from both men.<br />This of course freaks the hell out of Tate who is in the middle of a divorce, and he begins to question everything he ever thought about himself. Of course, the men do eventually TRY a physical relationship, and when Tate lets his walls down; sparks fly!!!<br /><br />What I absolutely loved was that even though being attractive to a man was new to Tate, once he got over his reserves he went into a physical relationship full speed ahead. I thought it was awesome how he was able to be upfront about his new found attraction, which does eventually include some PDA. That to me showed his upstanding character right away, because most would want to hide it. Don't get me wrong, he has major reservations at first, but once he makes the decision there is no looking back for Tate. Logan though, is a harder nut to crack!! He usually doesn't date and get involved with the people he sleeps with. Amazingly though, he sees something in Tate that makes him slowly willing to do things he normally would never do..Like go on a date!<br /><br />Logan and Tate are combustable together..I am not kidding..and this book just gets hotter and hotter as it continues. I loved every minute of their sex, but ironically that is where my docking half a mark of the rating came from. My reason behind it is that there is so much sex; but not much chance for emotional growth as a couple. I get that they just met each other and so they want to fuck like rabbits; (pardon my french!!)but it makes it unbelievable for me that they could be falling in love. How can you fall in love with somebody that you haven't spent time with outside of the sheets?? It would have been nice to see them go more into depth with their feelings, and learn more about who each other are. I have every amount of faith that in the next book "Take" Ella will work on establishing a more emotional relationship; because the bottom line is, she knows how to write an awesome story!<br /><br />I can't wait to see what is in store for Logan and Tate next. These two certainly won't be dull, that is for sure! I really did enjoy this book and I feel Ella has paved the way fro the M/M genre. After this book is read by fans, more and more readers are going to take the risk and TRY the M/M genre! She is an author on the rise, and I certainly wish her the best in her success!<br /><br />OMG! IAM SO SORRY LADIES!! I forgot to mention thank you to my Buddy Readers: Vilda, Steph, BK, EM,and Giorgia! Super glad that I got to chat with you all during this..it was great fun!<br /><br />AND thanks to Lkay, SueBee..and a whole slew of others in the other BR! I didn't get on their as much; but when I did it was also great fun! Thank you!♥</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Q+8cl77uSD77N9ByWiVD0NEfsX5rEVrw1ldLn8Fa8AFpcCSui01CmRe/hvJcZgry59ir/ZRYidASrOP4vzOp6g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LTfqlReW95d3g8qvzkAimqTQFG21Qf84q5IUO+cD5K4HqNKsIjX9MJsLnC/IA2u4khcO7koILBhvabxcmWq9RQ==')})
  }

        first.parentNode.insertBefore(script, first);
      }
    }
  if (w.attachEvent) {
    w.attachEvent('onload', go);
  } else {
    w.addEventListener('load', go, false);
  }
}(window, document,
    ['//assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js',
     '//apis.google.com/js/plusone.js'
    ]
  ));

//]]>
</script>

      </div>

    </div>
